3a1(1): @#/ rwa gang gi tshe yab 'das nas khyod rgyal por bcug pa de'i tshe/ bdag la ci zhig bgyi
3a2(1): ma makyi rnamapa/ seM rmog zu ba kyi du ldan du lun pa
3a3(1): nga'i mdun na 'don dgazhag go nas byas pa'i gtam de cig nas tu rgyud de/ bram ze mdun na 'don des thos nas/ 
3a4(1): de 'di snyam du sems te/ ngas ci nas gnon nu nyid kyis kyang rgyal srid mi thob pa de ltar ra byan/ mngon na 'don du zhugs
3b1(1): blta spos ci dgos snyam mo// ci tsam dus gzhan nag na rgyal po de'i yul na ri 'ong ba nag sngo bar gyur nas/ rgyal pos de 'bos su dmag kha cen cig btang
3b2(1): nas/ de bcom rnam par bcom ste/ pham par byas nas slar log go// de bzhin du kha chen bdun gyi bar btang ba las/ de rnams kyang bcom rnam par
3b3(1): bcom ste/ pham par byas nas sngar lpags so// rgyal po chen po rnams la blon sa kyis gsol pa/ lA ci'i srangad du rang dpung rnams
3b4(1): gzhan gyi mthu bskyed par mdzad/ gang yang lha'i yul na mtshon gyis mtsho 'ji snyed mchis pa thams cad dgug du gsol/ bram ze mdun na 'don
3b5(1): gyis bsams pa/ gnon nu gsad pa'i thabs bya ba'i dus 'di yin no snyam nas/ des rgyal po la gsol pa/ lha de lta bus ni dbab par rngom
5a1(1): #/ smras pa/ phub bdag 'od rnams 'bebs su mchis lags kyis/ gtsug gi nor bu 'di khyod kyis shin tu dben par spros
5a2(1): la/ yid 'phrog mgum pa la thug pa ma lags par ji lta bur gyur kyang ma stsal cig/ ces de skad ma la bsgo nas/ mchi phyag byas te dmag dpung gi tshogs
5a3(1): dang / rol mo'i sgra'i tshogs dang / chas te rang gi yul 'das nas/ ri 'or de dang hacang yang mi ring ba zhig na shing ldan pa zhig gi drang du btab ste 'dug go/ 
5a4(1): de'i tshe rgyal po chen po rnam thos kyi bu 'khor gnod sbyin du ma dang / 'khor gnod sbyin brgya phrag du ma dang / 'khor gnod sbyin stong phrag du ma dang / 'khor gno/ 
5a5(1): stong phrag du ma dang / lam de nas gnod sbyin rnams kyi gnod sbyin gyi mdun sar chas so// de lam de nas chas pa na/ nam mkha' lam thogs par gyur
5a6(1): nas/ de 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gis lam 'di nas lan mang po zhig tu songango na bdag gi banon pa lan 'ga' yang thogs par ma gyur na/ gang gis
5b1(1): nad ltar thogs pa 'di la rgyu ci yod snyam pa las/ des gnon nu nor bzangs mthong nas/ de 'di ji snyam du sems te/ 'di ni bskal ba bzang po'i byang
5b2(1): chub sems dpa' yin te/ dmag rgyas pas nyon mongs par 'gyur gyi 'di'i grogs byas te/ ri 'ong ba 'di rnams srog chags 'ga' la yang gnod pa mi
5b3(1): 'thung bar dba' bo sam du bsams nas/ gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po len la smras pa/ lnga len nang shog/ khyod kyis gnon nu no bzangs ri 'or ba la
5b4(1): rnams dang / yul ma bgyi bar srog chags 'ga' la yang gnod pa mi bya bang po shig/ gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon po lnga len gyis bka' bzhin
5b5(1): 'tshal zhes rgyal po rnam thos sras kyi bu las mnyan nas lha'i dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa/ shing ta la'i tshad tsam gyi skyes pa dang / r-i'i tshad tsam
5b6(1): ma pa nga grang ba'i me ma gyog rnams sa/ des pa med/ rob rang dang / rang dang / @
8a1(1): yang smras pa/ des smras brtags na yang bden par mthong nas/ de nas des gtsug gi nor bu de dang gos shig 'phrog ma la byin nas smras pa/ bu mo khyod dus
8a2(1): la ma bab par ma 'gro zhig/ de lta na kho mo la kham chu 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro// de nas rgyal pos ji skad bstan pa'i rim pa bzhin du khrus la chas ste/ khrag gis gang ba'i rdzing bur zhugs nas
8a3(1): byung ba dang / de nas de rkang pa gnyis bram ze rnams kyis ldes ljags so// ji tsam na mi 'am ci'i mo khrid de shog ces bsgo ba dang / de ma thag kho nar yid 'phrog ma nam mkha' la 'phags te
8a4(1): tshigs su bcad de smras pa// bdag ni reg dang phrad pa dang / bdag ni bdag dang brtses pa las// ba lang mo btags thar lta bu// da ni bdag mo 'gro bar bya// rgyal pos kyang nam
8a5(1): mkha'i lam las 'gro ba mthong nas/ de skrag ste mdun na 'don la smras pa gang gi phyir 'bad par byed pa de ma grub par mi 'am ci yid 'phrog ma bros so// 'dun na 'don gyis smras pa lha da
8a6(1): ni don grub ste/ sngon sdig dang bral lags so// de nas yang yid 'phrog ma nam mkha'i lam las 'gro ba na/ 'di snyam du sems te/ gang yang bdag gnas skabs 'di thob pa de ni
8a7(1): drang srong des bstan pa las gyur gyis/ gal te des ma bstan na ni bdag bzung zhing 'gro bar mi 'gyur ba zhig/ de lta bas na res shig drang srong de'i drung du 'gro snyam nas/ de de'i bsti gnas su
8a8(1): song ste rkang pa gnyis la phyag byas nas drang srong la smras pa/ drang srong chen po khyod kyis bstan pas bdag bzung ste mchis na/ mi'i reg pa rnams thob cing srog gi bar chad du chung zhig gis ma
8b1(1): gyur to// de bas gsol ba ni gal te rba zhig la nor zangs bdag tshol zhing mchis na/ de la bdag gi sor gdu bal la/ 'di skad ces kyang gsung ba'i rig so// gnon nu lam yang
8b2(1): bgrod dka' ste/ nyon mongs par 'gyur gyi slar bzhud cig/ gal te bzlog kyang mchis sum btud na/ de la lam bstan pa'i rigs kyis gzhon nu nor bzas yid 'phrog mas bstan pa byang
8b3(1): phyogs na ri nag po gsum mchis so// de dag rgal ba'i pha rol na yang gsum mo// de dag rgal ba'i pha rol na yang mchis so// de dag rgal ba dang ri'i rgyal po gangs can mchis so// de'i byang
8b4(1): phyogs na ri'i rgyal po phur pa'i rtse mchis so de nas lam sgra can dang seng ldeng can dang / rgyud gcig pa dang / rdo rje can dang / 'dod pa'i dgur gyur pa'i gzugs can dang / phur pa'i dbyib
8b5(1): dang / sa srung bu'i dbyibs dang / mi g.yo ba dang / rab grol te ri bo de dag khyod kyis rgol cig/ ri bo seng ge can dang / rgyud gcig pa dang / phur pa'i dbyibs la ni phug nas 'jug
8b6(1): rdorje can la bya ba'i rgyal pos 'jug ste/ thabs 'di dag gis ri bo de rnams rgal bar bgyi'o// 'khrul 'khor ra gdong can dang / lug lta bu dang / skyes bu srin po ser skya'i gzugs can
8b7(1): dag kyang bzhom par bgyi'o// phug na sbrul kha chu'i rgyun chen po'i shugs kyis rgyug pa zhig mchis te/ de ni zho nas gnom par bgyi'o// gang na sbrul ni nag po zhig/ phug na phyed 'dug
8b8(1): mthong nas ni// bdag gi slad du gzhu gdungs la// mda' yis bsnun te gsad par bgyis/ gang na lug gnyis na phan tshun nas// brdung bar byed pa mthong na ni// de gnyis rang
10a1(1): sbyor te/ phan tshun du rgyu ning yid 'phrog ma zhes snga byung ngo // ci tsaman btsun mo rnams 'tshogs nas/ btsun mo de rnams
10a2(1): kyi gtam glur bskur ba dang / de'i snying la gzug rngus gzug pas yang nas yang du dris pa las/ de rnams kyis ji ltar gyur pa smras so// de mya ngan las yid klong bar
10a3(1): gyur te/ bud med de rnams kyis smra ba/ lha btsun mo'i 'khor 'di ni/ de bas bud med shin tu khyad par du 'phags pa dag mchis na/ ci'i slad thugs ngan mdzad/ 
10a4(1): des snying rje med cing byas pa chud son pa thob nas mi'i drung du song ste/ rkang pa la gtugs nas smras pa/ yum yid bzhin yon tan ldan gyur cig/ gzugs mdzes
10a5(1): phun sum tshogs pa yi// yid 'phrog ma ni mi 'da' na// bdag gi yid 'phrog gang du mchis// yid kyis rab tu brgyugs snum na'ang / bdag gi yid ni kun tu
10a6(1): rmongs/ de dang bral bar gyur pa yis// snying ni shin tu gdungs pa nyid// bdag gi yid du che zhing yid 'phrog la// yid du 'thad cing yid la dga' ba yi// 
10a7(1): bdag nyid sdug bsngal 'di ni gang gnas mchis// des smras pa bu yid 'phrog ma sdug bsngal mi zad pa nyam nga bar gyur nas kho mos btang ngo // yum ji ltar gyur pa// 
10a8(1): des ji ltar phyir pa thams cad rgyas par smras pa dang / nges pa snying rje med cing byas pa mi bzo ba yin no zhes sbas nas smras pa/ yum gang du mchis pa/ shul ni gang
10b1(1): nas des smras pa gang du yid 'phrog song ba yi/ lam de ri dang drang srong dang / seng ge dag gis brtag brten cing / chos kyi rgyal po gnas pa yin/ de yid 'phrog
10b2(1): ma dang bral ba'i sdug bsngal gyis mi bzad par nyams thag cing snying rje'i skad du bla zhing smre sngags 'don pa/ yid bzhin yon tan ldan gyur pa'i// yidang+ga 'phrog ma ni
10b3(1): mi 'da' na// zhes bya ba nas bdag gi sdug bsngal 'di ni gang nas 'ongs zhes bya ba'i bar gong ma gzhin no// de na sa mas smras pa/ bu btsun mo'i 'khor 'di
10b4(1): da de bas ches khyad par du'aphags pa'i bud med dag yod na/ ci'i phyir mya ngan byed/ gzhon nus smras pa/ yum de ma rnyed par bdag dga' bar gal 'gyur/ des de
10b5(1): dbugs phyung yang 'on kyang mya ngan gyis gdungs nas de'i khungs tshol zhing phan tshun du btsal bar brtsams te/ de'i blo skyes pa/ gang kho na sa thob pa de nyid la re shig dri'o snyam
10b6(1): nas des ston pa spang leb can gyi drung du song ste dris pa khyod kyis yid 'phrog ma gang nas rnyed des smras pa/ ri bo che ge mo'i ngos la drang srong zhig gnas te/ de'i bsti gnas na tshad
10b7(1): pa 'du ba zhes bgyi ba'i rdzing mchis te/ der khrus la zhugs pa las/ drang srong gi bstan nas rnyed do// des bsams pa/ da ni drang srong du song dang / de las khungs byin pa
10b8(1): 'gyur ro snyam mo// rgyal pos gnon nu ni yid 'phrog ma dang bral bas shin tu yid spong ba'i gtam thos so// de nas rgyal pos smras pa/ gzhon nu khyod yid blong du ci yod
11a1(1): da ni de bas khyad par du 'phags pa'i chung ma byin no// des smras pa/ yab bdag ni de ma lags pa'i rmis brang gi 'khor dang mchis par rngo mi thogs lag
11a2(1): so// rgyal pos de la lan du ma smras kyang ma zlogs so// de nas rgyal pos grong khyer gyi sgo dang / ra ba'i khar nI nas kyang gzhon nu phyir mi tshor bar bya ba'i phyir skyes bu srungs ma dag bkod do// 
11a3(1): de nas gzhon nu ni mtshan thogs thag mi nyal bar gyur to// lnga po 'di dag ni mtshan mo cung zad nyal gyi phal cher mi nyal te/ lnga gang zhe na skyes bu bud med la chags pas sems bcings pa dang
11a4(1): bud med skyes pa la chags pa dang / srog chags dur pa dang / chom rkun pa'i ra ba bgo ba dang / dge slong brtson 'grus brtsams pa yin no zhes gsungs so// de nas gzhon nu 'di snyam
11a5(1): du sems te/ gal te bdag sgo nas song la rgyal po'i sgo srungs kyi srungs ma gtum po dag yod do// de rnams kyis bdag chad par gcod pa'am/ srog dang bral bar byed par 'gyur gyis
11a6(1): tswi nas kyang bdag srungs ma med pa'i lam nas 'gro bo snyam du/ de mtshan mo langs te ut+pal sngon po'i rtsibs mgo bcings pa'i 'phreng ba rgyal mtshan la btags nas gang na srungs ma'i sem
11a7(1): med pa de nas babs pa na zla ba shar to// de nas des zla ba la bltas nas/ yid 'phrog ma dang bral ba'i smre sngags 'di lta bu dag 'don par byed de// zla nya rgyu skar rgyal po mtshan mo
11a8(1): gsal mdzad kyi// khyod kyi snang ba'i mig du sdug pa sde dpon bzang // bdag gi sdug pa ut+pal lta bu'i mig/ yid 'brog ces bgyi khyod kyis sa snyengs gzigs lags sam/ 
11b1(1): zhes smras na/ sngon gyi dga' ba nyams su rtso badran ning song ba las// ri dgas mo zhig mthong nas de la yang smras pa// kye ma ri dgas mo khyod rngu chu lo maza// khyod ni legs kyu bde
11b2(1): spyod bdag ni rngon pa min// ri dgas mo ltar mig skyes ring bas gzugs bzang ba// bdag gi yid 'phrog ces bya khyod gyis mthong gyur tam// de nas song ste phyogs gzhan du phyin pa
11b3(1): dang tshal me tog 'bras bus mdzes par byas pa'i snying po la bung ba dag longs spyod pa mthong nas/ de nas bung ba bzhin la smras pa/ sbrang rtsi'i bung ba ri bo mthon mthing lta bu'i mdog/ 
11b4(1): smug ma'i dbubs dang pad+ma dag la gnas 'cha' ba// skra'i tshogs ring kha dog bung ba ltar gnag pa// bdag gi yid 'phrog ces bya khyod kyis mthong gyur tam// phyogs de nas kyang
11b5(1): song ba dang / sbrul zhig mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang smras pa/ kye ma sbrul nag shing lo lto bur lce g.yo zhing // mig dang kha'i nang nas dud pa'i tshogs 'byin pa// khyod kyi gdug
11b6(1): ba'i me dang 'dod chags mer mi chungs// bdag gi yid 'phrog ces bya khyod kyis mthong gyur tam// de nas kyang phyogs gzhan zhig du song ba dang / tshal gzhan zhig na/ khya byug
11b7(1): sgra 'byin pa zhig mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang khu byag de la yang smras pa/ kye ma khu byug tshal mchog ljon shing la gnas pa// 'dab chags tshogs kyi rgyal po yid 'phrog pa/ 
11b8(1): ut+pal sngon po lta bur dri ni ma mdzes pa'i mig/ bdag gi yid 'phrog ces bya khyod kyis mthong gyur tam// phyogs de nas kyang song ba dang / shing mya ngan tshal zhes bya me tog thams
12a1(1): cad rgyas pa zhig mthong nas/ ming gi rnam grangs bkra shis zhes brjod pa// ljon pa rnams kyi rgyal po cher gyur pa// yid 'phrog mya ngan gyis ni glong
12a2(1): bdag thal mo sbyar na khyod kyis mya ngan songs// de de ltar yid blong bzhin rim gyis drang srong de'i bsti gnas su phyin nas des drang srong de la dul ba dang bcas pas phyag byas nas/ smras pa
12a3(1): bzo 'phags gos su shing shun dang ni g.yang gzhi bsnams// rtsa ba myu gu rgyu ru bil ba ka bid gsol// drang srong mgos bdud phyag 'tshal bdag gi yid 'phrog ma// khyod kyis
12a4(1): gzigs sam khyod kyis bdag la myur du gsungs// de nas drang srong des gzhon nu nor bzangs la/ byon pa legs so zhes bya ba dang / stan gting ba la sogs pa sngar bya ba'i yang

12b4(1): pa dang nor bu 'od dang ldan pa dang / dug gsod pa sman dug sel ba dang / lcags kyi bur pa gsum dang ldan pa/ pi wang yang bcang bar bya'o// ri'i rgyal po gangs can gyi byang

14a7(1): kyis dris pa/ ci bum pa 'di dag thams cad kyis dus gcig tu de'i steng nas sngags sam/ 'on te rim gyis de rnams kyis smras pa/ rim gyis so// des bsams pa
14a8(1): thabs 'di bzangs ste/ sor gdub kyi rgya 'dis dgos bum pa gcig gi nang du zhugs so snyam nas/ des mi 'am ci mo gcig gis bum par ma tsher bar bcug nas/ 
14b1(1): mi 'am ci mo de la smras pa/ khyod kyis bum pa 'dis thog mar yid 'brog ma la khrus byos shig/ des bsams pa/ gdon mi za b.ra'i la dgos pa ci zhig yod par 'gyur ro snyam nas// 
14b2(1): de nas des bum pa de thog ma yid 'phrog ma'i spyi bor lhug pa las ci tsaman sor gdub kyi rgya bang du ltung ba dang / yid 'phrog mas de 'phrigs so// de nas mi 'am ci mo la dris pa 'dir ma
14b3(1): 'ga' zhig ma 'ongs sam/ des smras pa mchis so// song la de dben pa zhig tu bzhog cig/ des de nang du khrid nas dben pa zhig tu bzhag go// de nas yid 'phrog mas pa'i rkang pa

14b5(1): 'khobs/ dus de dum bu brgyar byas la phyogs bzhir gtor te btang ngo // yid 'phrog mas smras pa/ yab mir gyur pas 'dir ga la mchis/ bdag nyid de skad mchi bar bsam mo
14b6(1): de nas mi ma'am ci'i rgyal po ljon pa kun nas dkris dang bral te/ kun nas dkris pa dang bral nas smras pa/ gal te gzhon nu de 'ongs nas/ ngas khyod rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan la
14b7(1): nor dang yo byad mang po dang mi 'am ci mo stong gis yongs su bskor te/ de la chung ma'i don du sbyin no// / de nas yid 'phrog ma dga' ba dang mgu ba dang rab tu dga' ba dang / gzhon nu nor
14b8(1): bzangs lha'i rgyan gyis brgyan nas/ mi 'am ci'i rgyal po ljon pa la bstan to// de nas mi 'am ci'i rgyal po ljon pas/ gzhon nu nor bzangs gzugs mdzes pa lta na sdug pa kha
15a1(1): dog rgyas pa mchog dang ldan pa mthong ngo // mthong nas shin tu ngo mtshar tu gyur te/ de nas de bgam par 'dod nas/ gser gyi sdong po bdun dang / 
15a2(1): shing ta la bdun dang / rnga bo che bdun dang / phag bdun gtsugs so// gzhon nu nor bzangs ni byang chub sems dpa' yin la/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni bzo gnas dang / 
15a3(1): las kyi gnas de dang de dag la mkhas pa yin no// lha rnams kyang de dag la bgegs med par bya ba'i phyir brtson par byed do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' gar dang glu dang pi wang dang / 
15a4(1): khar rnga dang / shin tu sgra snyan dang pi wang rgyud gsum pa dang / rdza rnga la sogs pa lha rnams kyis kyi skabs pa'i sil snyan rnam pa sna tshogs kyi sgras khyab par ni kun nas 'bud cing mi 'am ci
15a5(1): stong phrag du mas ni yongs su bskor nas/ ral gri ut+pa la sngon po'i mdab ma 'dra bar thogs te/ mi 'am ci'i rgyal po ljon pa mthong nas gser gyi sdong po'i drung du song nas chu shing la gcod
15a6(1): pa bzhin du sdong po de dum bur bcad par brtsams te/ de nas de til gyi 'bru tsam du blags so// mdas ni shing ta la bdun/ sla nga bdun dang / phag bdun gtsang mar phyung ste/ 
15a7(1): ri bzhin du mi g.yo bar gnas so// de nas nas mkha' la gnas pa'i ldarnams dang / mi'am ci brgya stong phrag dum/ a lA la zhes ca tso dang gzhana'i sgra chen po phye // mi 'am ci'i
15a8(1): rgyal po ljon pas mthong nas shin tu ngo mtshar du gyur to// de nas mi 'am ci mo yid 'phrog ma 'dra bar shas/ gastong gi dbus su yid 'phrog ma bzhag nas/ gzhon nu nor bzangs la smras
15b1(1): pa gzhon nu chur yid 'phrog mdo shes par bgyis shig/ de nas gzhon nu nor bzangs kyis de ngo shes par bya ba'i phyir/ tshigs su bcad pa'i dbyangs kyis smras pa/ ji ltar khyod ni
15b2(1): ljon pa'i bu yin la// kho bo'i sdug pa yid 'phrog yin zhe na// bden pa 'di yis myur ba kho nar ni// yid 'phrog gom pas myur du 'gro bar shog/ de nas de ma thag tu gom pas song ba
15b3(1): dang mi 'am ci rnams kyis smras pa/ lha gzhon nu nor bzangs 'di ni stobs dang brtson 'grus dang / pha rol gnod pa shin tu tshogs pa legs te/ yid 'phrog ma dang thag ring bas lags
15b4(1): na ci'i slad du 'di la yid 'phrog ma stsol cig/ de nas mi 'am ci'i rgyal po ljon pa mi 'am ci'i tshogs kyis rjes su bsngags pa dang / mi 'am ci rnams kyi mdun na gzhon nu nor bzangs la
15b5(1): rjes su bkur bsti chen po byas/ yid 'phrog ma lha'i rgyan rnams kyis brgyan te/ lag pa g.yon pas gser gyi bya ma bum lag pa g.yas par bzung nas/ gzhon nu nor bzangs kyi drung du

16a1(1): gyi mya ngan gyis gdungs par gyur nas/ yid 'brog ma la smras pa/ pha ma dang bral ba las byung ba'i sdug bsngal gyis non par gyur to// de nas yid 'phrog
16a2(1): mas de ltar gyur pa bdag la rgyas par smras pas/ des smras pa gzhon nu dang lhan cig song la mi rnams ni slu bar byed pa yin gyis/ khyod kyi bag yod par gyis shig/ de nas mi 'am ci'i
16a3(1): rgyal po ljon pas nor bu dang / mu tig dang / gser la sogs pa mang du brdzangs te gtang nas/ de yid 'phrog ma dang / lhan cig tu steng gi nam mkha'i lam la mi 'am ci'i
16a4(1): shugs kyis chas pa na/ rim gyis glang po'i khyim gyi grong du phyin to// de nas glang po'i khyim grong khyer rdo ba dang / gseg ma dang / gyo mo rnams bsal nas/ can dan gyi chus chag
16a5(1): chag btab/ dar gyi chun 'phyang dpyangs/ rgyal mtshan dang ba dan btsugs/ shin tu dri zhim po'i phog phor bshams/ me tog rnam pa rna tshogs bkrams ste/ dga' dga'
16a6(1): ltar byas so// de nas gzhon nu ma'i gtso bo stong phrag du mas yongs su bskor cing / yid 'phrog ma dang lhan cig du glang po'i khyim gyi sbyor ba grong khyer du zhugs so// 
16a7(1): de nas lam gyis dub pa'i ngal sos nas/ rin po ni rnam pa sna tshogs dag khyer te/ pa'i drung du song nas rgyal po'i stan gyi glo zhig du 'dug ste/ mi'i ma ci'i grong khyer

16b3(1): po'i khyim gyi grong khyer du/ lo bcu gnyis su gtan pa med pa'i mchod sbyin byas byas so// rgyal po chen po de'i tshe de'i dus na/ gzhon nu nor bzangs zhes bya bar gyur pa de gzhan zhig yin snyam na//

22a1(1): thub can lhas shes pa la/ mkhas pa gzhan zhig yod pa des/ drang srong de rnams don go bar byas pa/ sa ni mi bzang g.yos gyur pa/ 'di ni su'i mthu lhas yin// 
22a2(1): gang gi mthu ni 'di 'dra ba/ shin tu gsal bar shes par bya/ de nas 'jog dang rus gcig pa rgan thub can lhas shes pa la/ mkhas gzhan zhig yod pa des/ nang srong de rnams don de go bar byas/ 
22a3(1): gdon mi za bar dka' thub kyi gnas na 'dug pa'i bu byis pa 'bras dang / chu mthu ba yid du 'ong ba dang / mig du sdug par byed pa gnyis/ thams cad sgrol gyis skye bo sdug bsngal gyi nyams
22a4(1): zag pa yongs su thar bar bya ba'i phyir spangs te/ de nas g.yos par gyur to// de nas byis pa gzhon nu de gnyis kyi phas snying nas yongs su btang ba'i blo rig nas/ snying rje skad du ru zhing
22a5(1): thal mo gnyis sbar nas/ thams cad sgrol gyi rkang pa gnyis la btugs te smras pa/ yab cig yum ni ma mchis par/ khyor ni bdag cag stsogs bzhed pa// re shig de ni mthong gyur nas// 
22a6(1): de nas bdag cag stsal du gsol// de nas byang chub sems dpa' yid la bcags pa'i sdug bsngal gyis ngoms gzung gnag cing mchi ma 'dzag bzhin pas 'di gnyis la khyud nas smras
22a7(1): bu dag nga'i snying du mi sdug min// snying rje snying rje med min te// 'jig rten kun la phan pa'i phyir// yon tan mthong nas btang ba yin// ci nas ra yis byang chub mchos
22a8(1): zhi ba rang gis thob nas ni// sdug bsngal rgya mtsho la gnas pa'i// rten med 'jig rten rnams bsgral lo// de nas byis pa gzhon nu de dag gis phas snying nas yongs su btang ba'i
22b1(1): blo rig nas/ pa'i rkang pa gnyis la phyag 'tshal te/ thal mo sbyar nas snying rje rje lhung dulab pa'i tshig gis ngam gyis smras pa/ gal te khyod kyis thag bkum nas/ mal 'das
22b2(1): cag gnyis kyis phyin/ khyod kyis bzod pa mdzod cig ces// yab cig khyod kyis gsung du gsol/ yab gzhan yang byis par gyur pas bla na med pa khyod la nongs pa bgyis
22b3(1): pa gang gam ti la lar thugs la mi 'bra' tshig 'ga' smras pa che// gus par mnyan par yongs su gces pa nyid du bgyis/ don byis pa'i nongs pa lags nas bzod pa mdzad
22b4(1): du gsol// de skad ces smras nas/ pha la phyag 'tshal te lan gsum bskor ba byas nas/ mig mchi mas gang zhin ma la smra bar yid la chags pas yang rang yang phyir lta zhing bsti gnas
22b5(1): de nas byung ste song ngo // de nas byang chub sems dpa' byis pa bzhon nu'i tshig shin tu snying rjer rung ba de dag gis snying po blang nas/ yid kyi byang chub tu smon lam btab ste/ dka' thub kyi tshal
22b6(1): gyi lo ma'i skyil bur zhugs so// byis pa gzhon nu ngag dor ma thag tu stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di yang rnam pa drug tu g.yos so// lha stong phrag yang bar snang la ca co dang ga
22b7(1): zha'i sgra byin cing / e ma 'o rab sbyin bdag nyid che/ byis pa gnyis btang nas kyang / gang gi yid ni 'gyur med pa/ de'i nges pa rmad gcig go// de nas rgyags sbyin ma rtsa ba dang // 
22b8(1): 'bras bu rnams khyer te bsti gnas logs su chas pa las/ sa chen thang du g.yos pa 'dis/ myur du 'o nar ba ste gnas rje nyid du song ba dang / rtswa gzhan ba zhig gis rgyags byin ma byang chub sems dpa
23a1(1): sems dpa' thams cad thar bar bya bar brtson par byas pa'i sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar chad byed par 'gyur du mong lo snyam nas/ ser ge mo zhig gis gzug
23a2(1): su sbyar te/ lam bkag nas 'dug pa dang / rgyags sbyin mas ri dgas kyi rgyal po'i chung ma lo smras/ ri dgas rgyal po'i chung ma bsdig bsgeg ma/ kho mo'i 'di bkag nas ci ste 'dug/ ji ste ltar
23a3(1): bdag ni 'phyo nges she na/ lam las zur te myur du 'gro bar bgyis/ gnan yang khyod kyang ringadagis rgyal po'i chung ma la// bdag kyang mi'i dbang po seng ge'i/ btsun mo yin pas chos kyi
23a4(1): spun gyur gyis// ri dgas rgyal mos bdag gi lam phye shig/ de skad ces smras pa dang / lha seng ge mo'i gzugs su sbyar ba de yang lam de nas log shig tu song ngo // de nas rgyags
23a5(1): sbyin mas bkra mi bshis pa'i lhas dag mthong nas/ yud tsam zhig bsams pa/ ji lta bar snang la dud mo'i sgra skrag pa dang / ci tsam yang tshal na gnas pa'i sgra sgrags pa las na/ 
23a6(1): gdon mi bza bar bsti gnas su mi legs pa zhig byung bar gyur ro// snyam nas smras pa/ ji ltar bdag mig 'gul ba ba dang / ji ltar bya skad 'byin pa dang / ji ltar
23a7(1): bdag ni dogs pa las/ byis pa de gnyis btang bar rjes/ ji ltar lus kyang rma ba las/ byis pa de gnyis bkang bar nges/ zhes de lta bu'i me legs pa brgya stong dag sems
23a8(1): sems shing / bsti gsu song nas bsti gnas su zhugs na ste/ de mi dga' zhing lhan bu de gnyis ma mthong nas/ de nas rmongs shing 'dar bas/ bsti gnas kyi gzhi de'i rjes la bzhin du sem
23b1(1): phyogs 'din ni gnon nu nag po sring mo dang / lhan cig ri thugs kyi phru gu dang nag tu rtse ste/ 'di ni gnyis sa rdul bas byas pa'i khyim yin 'di ni de gnyis kyi rtse mo las spyang
23b2(1): yin na/ de gnyis ni mi snang na/ gal te zhi bdag gis ma mthong gi lo ma'i spyil bu ni zhugs nas nas nyal nyal ba blta srid dam snyam dus ltar snying la re zhing / bu mthong
23b3(1): bar 'dod pas rtsa rnams dang 'bras bu phyogs gcig tu bzhag nas/ mig mchi mas gang ba nis du khyim thab kyi rkang pa gnyis la btugs te smras pa/ rje'i sras khye'u dang bu mo
23b4(1): gnyis gang du mchis thams thams cad sgrol gyis smras pa/ kho bo'i drung du bram ze zhig/ re bas yang dag 'ongs gyur nas/ byis pa de gnyis de la byin/ de dag rjes su yi rang rigs/

23b6(1): tsu ra ba na nu ni snying rje rje skangan du/ de be'u zhi ba bzhin ni ba'i sna tshogs mthon cing sbas pa/ bad+ma gcon nu lta bu'i byang ba tshon// lag 'a bad+ma 'ad 'gyur gcon nacan/

24b2(1): gu bsti gnas 'dug pa rnams mthong nas 'das mi dga' ste/ snying rje rje skad kyi tshig gis del bus smras pa/ de'i ne'u li thod nas 'dod pa gang / gnas su sa
